remarks:        +==============================================================+
remarks:        | Some BGP COMMUNITIES of Transroute |
remarks:        +--------------------------------------------------------------+
remarks:        | Common syntax: |
remarks:        | |
remarks:        | 50509:VCNN (info) |
remarks:        | |
remarks:        | where fields are: |
remarks:        | |
remarks:        | V - Info about route: |
remarks:        | 4 - ipv4 |
remarks:        | 6 - ipv6 |
remarks:        | |
remarks:        | C - Source/Destination class |
remarks:        | 1 - UpStream |
remarks:        | 2 - Private Peering |
remarks:        | 4 - Customer |
remarks:        | 6 - Groups |
remarks:        | 7 - IX COMMON |
remarks:        | 8 - IX DIRECT |
remarks:        | 9 - IX RS route |
remarks:        | 699 - ALL |
remarks:        | |
remarks:        | NN - Number of Neighbor within class |
remarks:        | |
remarks:        +==============================================================+
remarks:        | UpStreams (C=1) |
remarks:        | 06 - Cogent |
remarks:        | 07 - ReTN |
remarks:        | 13 - RASCOM |
remarks:        | 15 - Beeline |
remarks:        | 19 - HE.net |
remarks:        | 20 - Rostelecom |
remarks:        | 22 - TIS |
remarks:        | 23 - Fiord |
remarks:        | 33 - DDoS Guard |
remarks:        | 34 - InterLink |
remarks:        | 99 - ALL |
remarks:        |..............................................................|
remarks:        | Directs (C=2) |
remarks:        | 18 - Melbicom |
remarks:        | 19 - Rutube |
remarks:        | 20 - Mnogobyte |
remarks:        | 21 - CDNvideo |
remarks:        | 22 - Mediaoperator |
remarks:        | 99 - ALL |
remarks:        |..............................................................|
